# cart icon

# logout

```html
<div
  class="fhs_center_left fhs_mouse_point"
  style="border-top: 1px solid #F2F4F5;"
>
  <a class="fhs_center_left fhs_flex_grow" href="/customer/account/logout/"
    ><span class="ico_logout_gray" style="margin-right:8px;"></span
    ><span>Thoát tài khoản</span></a
  >
</div>
```

# add to cart

```html
<button
  type="button"
  title="Thêm vào giỏ hàng"
  class="btn-cart-to-cart"
  onclick="productAddToCartForm.submit(this); return false;"
>
  <span class="fhs_icon_cart"></span><span>Thêm vào giỏ hàng</span>
</button>
```

```html
<div
  style="border-radius:5px; height:200px; filter: alpha(opacity=80); background-color:black; opacity:0.85; display:flex; flex-direction:column;align-items:center; z-index:999999;width:414px !important; justify-content:center;"
  class="wrapper_box"
>
  <div>
    <img
      src="https://cdn1.fahasa.com/media/fahasa_web_image/add_to_cart_success_image_v2.png"
      style="width:100px; height:100px;"
    />
  </div>
  <br />
  <div>
    <p
      style="font-family:Nunito Sans; font-weight:bold; color:white; text-align:center; z-index:999999999;font-size:18px;"
    >
      Sản phẩm đã được thêm vào giỏ hàng.
    </p>
  </div>
</div>
```

# cart detail

```html
<div>
  <div class="header-cart-item" style="display: flex;">
    <div class="checkbox-all-product ">
      <input
        class="checkbox-add-cart"
        type="checkbox"
        id="checkbox-all-products"
        onclick="cart.checkAllProducts()"
      />
    </div>
    <div>
      <span
        >Chọn tất cả (<span class="num-items-checkbox">8</span> sản phẩm)</span
      >
    </div>
    <div>Số lượng</div>
    <div>Thành tiền</div>
    <div></div>
  </div>
  <div class="product-cart-left">
    <div class="item-product-cart">
      <div class="checked-product-cart">
        <input
          type="checkbox"
          id="checkbox-product-1047301"
          name="checkbox_product_1047301"
          class="checkbox-add-cart"
          onclick="cart.addCheckedProductToBuy('1047301')"
        />
      </div>
      <div class="img-product-cart">
        <a
          class="product-image"
          href="https://www.fahasa.com/cay-cam-ngot-cua-toi-tai-ban-2026.html"
          ><img
            src="https://cdn1.fahasa.com/media/catalog/product//i/m/image_217480_1.jpg"
            width="120"
```

# login

```html
<div>
  <button
    type="button"
    onclick="fhs_account.showLoginPopup('login');"
    title="Đăng nhập"
    class="fhs_btn_default active"
  >
    <span>Đăng nhập</span>
  </button>
</div>
```

```html
<div class="popup-login-content">
  <form class="fhs-login-form">
    <div class="fhs-input-box">
      <label>Số điện thoại/Email</label>
      <div class="fhs-input-group">
        <input
          class="fhs-textbox"
          type="text"
          placeholder="Nhập số điện thoại hoặc email"

          maxlength="200"
          name="youama-email"
          value=""
        />
        <span class="fhs-input-icon fhs-textbox-alert"></span>
      </div>
      <div class="fhs-input-alert"></div>
    </div>
    <div class="fhs-input-box fhs-input-display">
```
